\mbox{\Hypertarget{mxfdec_8c_a129747115417333151ed09675af02c4d}\label{mxfdec_8c_a129747115417333151ed09675af02c4d}} 
\index{mxfdec.c@{mxfdec.c}!mxf\_compute\_ptses\_fake\_index@{mxf\_compute\_ptses\_fake\_index}}
\index{mxf\_compute\_ptses\_fake\_index@{mxf\_compute\_ptses\_fake\_index}!mxfdec.c@{mxfdec.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mxf\_compute\_ptses\_fake\_index()}{mxf\_compute\_ptses\_fake\_index()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} mxf\+\_\+compute\+\_\+ptses\+\_\+fake\+\_\+index (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_m_x_f_context}{M\+X\+F\+Context}} $\ast$}]{mxf,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_m_x_f_index_table}{M\+X\+F\+Index\+Table}} $\ast$}]{index\+\_\+table }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

We have this\+:

x Temporal\+Offset 0\+: 0 1\+: 1 2\+: 1 3\+: -\/2 4\+: 1 5\+: 1 6\+: -\/2

We want to transform it into this\+:

x D\+TS P\+TS 0\+: -\/1 0 1\+: 0 3 2\+: 1 1 3\+: 2 2 4\+: 3 6 5\+: 4 4 6\+: 5 5

We do this by bucket sorting x by x+\+Temporal\+Offset\mbox{[}x\mbox{]} into mxf-\/$>$ptses, then settings mxf-\/$>$first\+\_\+dts = -\/\mbox{\hyperlink{cuda__runtime_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max(\+Temporal\+Offset\mbox{[}x\mbox{]})}}. The latter makes D\+TS $<$= P\+TS.
